# Initial setup and startup
ms_setup = {
	# Delete units
	msw_kill_units = yes

	# Set province ids for ambient objects
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = game_start_setup }
		}
		MSW = {
		    set_variable = { which = msw_id value = 0 }
		    minesweeper_region = {
		        set_variable = { which = msw_id which = PREV }
		        PREV = { change_variable = { which = msw_id value = 1 } }
		    }
		}
	}

	# Fix treasury
	msw_reset_cash = yes

	# Fix TI
	north_america = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	north_east_pacific_region = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	american_east_coast_region = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	caribbean_sea_region = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1658 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	4940 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	4941 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1922 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1906 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1903 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1905 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1904 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1907 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1910 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1908 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1909 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1659 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1660 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1661 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1662 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1663 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1664 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1911 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1665 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1917 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1916 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1919 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1918 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1920 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1912 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1913 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1916 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1921 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1914 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1923 = { undiscover_country = MSW }
	1582 = { discover_country = MSW }
	4999 = { discover_country = MSW }


	set_global_flag = game_start_setup
}

# Reset money to 10 ducats, to counter starting defecit
msw_reset_cash = {
	MSW = {
		while = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { treasury = 10 }
			}
			add_treasury = 400
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				treasury = 11
			}
			add_treasury = -1
		}
	}
}

# First wrapper for admin dev
msw_adm_dev_wrapper = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				region = minesweeper_region
				NOT = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
		ms_admin_clear = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ai = yes }
		add_adm_power = -5
	}
}

# Wrapper for diplo dev
msw_dip_dev_wrapper = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				region = minesweeper_region
				NOT = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
		ms_clear_all_adjacent_if_complete = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ai = yes }
		add_dip_power = -5
	}
}

# Wrapper for mil dev
msw_mil_dev_wrapper = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				region = minesweeper_region
				NOT = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
		ms_flag_province = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ai = yes }
		add_mil_power = -5
	}
}

# Kill all units in MSW/sea zone
msw_kill_units = {
	minesweeper_region = {
		kill_units = {
			who = owner
		}
	}
	1582 = {
		kill_units = {
			type = heavy_ship
		}
		kill_units = {
			type = light_ship
		}
		kill_units = {
			type = galley
		}
		kill_units = {
			type = transport
		}
	}
}

# Second wrapper for admin dev
ms_admin_clear = {
	# Wrapper for clear province through admin development (and not dip)
	# Has to be placed in a mid wrapper for admin dev specifically
	# If there is only 1 wrapper events will not show up
	owner = {
		add_adm_power = 5
	}
	add_base_tax = -1

	# This is the clear action
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag
		}
		ms_clear_province = yes
	}
}

# Clear a province
ms_clear_province = {
	# Bomb
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = bomb_flag
		}
		# The game is lost, fire an event indicating this

		owner = {
			country_event = {
				id = minesweeper.6
			}
		}

		# show every province on the board for its final color
		minesweeper_region = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = bomb_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = bomb_mod
					duration = -1
				}
				ms_show_bomb_tile_in_prov = yes
				clr_province_flag = bomb_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = zero_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = zero_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = zero_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_0_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = zero_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = one_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = one_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = one_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_1_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = one_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = two_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = two_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = two_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_2_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = two_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = three_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = three_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = three_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_3_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = three_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = four_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = four_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = four_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_4_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = four_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = five_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = five_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = five_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_5_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = five_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = six_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = six_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = six_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_6_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = six_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = seven_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = seven_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = seven_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_7_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = seven_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = eight_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = question_mod
					ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = eight_mod }
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = eight_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_8_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				clr_province_flag = eight_flag
			}
		}

		# Also mark off the game_in_progress_flag flag for the owner scope. This variable will unlock the "reset game" decision
		clr_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag

	}

	# Other Tiles
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = question_mod
		}
		# Province hasnt been clicked before
		# We should reveal the tile

		# Increase game score
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = score
				value = 1
			}
		}

		remove_province_modifier = question_mod
		ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = zero_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zero_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_0_tile_in_prov = yes

			ms_clear_all_0_tiles = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = one_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = one_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_1_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = two_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = two_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_2_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = three_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = three_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_3_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = four_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = four_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_4_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = five_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = five_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_5_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = six_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = six_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_6_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = seven_flag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = seven_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_7_tile_in_prov = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = eight_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_8_tile_in_prov = yes
		}

	}

	# Check win condition

	ms_win_condition = yes
	# if not any of the above do nothing
}

# Flag a province
ms_flag_province = {
	owner = {
		add_mil_power = 5
	}
	add_base_manpower = -1

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag
		}

		# This is the flag action
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = question_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = question_mod
			ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = flag_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes

			# increase score if it is a bomb province
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = bomb_flag
				}
				owner = {
					change_variable = {
						which = score
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}

			# increase flags placed variable
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = flags_placed
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = flag_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
			ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = question_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			ms_show_question_tile_in_prov = yes
			# decrease score if it is a bomb province
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = bomb_flag
				}
				owner = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = score
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}

			# decrease flags placed variable
			owner = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = flags_placed
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}

		ms_win_condition = yes
	}
}

# Check win condition and win the game
ms_win_condition = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = {
						which = score
						value = 100
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag
		owner = {
			country_event = {
				id = minesweeper.7
			}
		}
	}
}

# Middle-mouse click
ms_clear_all_adjacent_if_complete = {
	owner = {
		add_dip_power = 5
	}
	add_base_production = -1

	# Check if game in progress
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag
		}

		# Check if the interaction is valid
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = question_mod }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = zero_mod }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = flag_mod }
				}
			}
			# Then check if the province has as many flags as its number

			# Count number of flags
			set_variable = {
				which = dip_adj_flag_count
				value = 0
			}
			minesweeper_region = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					NOT = {
						province_distance = {
							who = PREV
							distance = 29
						}
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					change_variable = {
						which = dip_adj_flag_count
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}

			# Check if its as many as number
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 8
							}
							has_province_flag = eight_flag
						}

						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 7
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 8
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = seven_flag
						}

						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 6
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 7
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = six_flag
						}
						
						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 5
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 6
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = five_flag
						}
						
						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 4
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 5
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = four_flag
						}
						
						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 3
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 4
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = three_flag
						}
						
						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 2
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 3
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = two_flag
						}
						
						AND = {
							check_variable = {
								which = dip_adj_flag_count
								value = 1
							}
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = dip_adj_flag_count
									value = 2
								}
							}
							has_province_flag = one_flag
						}
					}
				}

				# Now, check if it has at least 1 uncleared (question_mod) neighbor

				minesweeper_region = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
						NOT = {
							province_distance = {
								who = PREV
								distance = 29
							}
						}
					}
					set_global_flag = dip_dev_clear_yes
				}

				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = dip_dev_clear_yes }
					clr_global_flag = dip_dev_clear_yes

					minesweeper_region = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = question_mod
							NOT = {
								province_distance = {
									who = PREV
									distance = 29
								}
							}
						}
						ms_clear_province = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#clear all tiles next to a 0 tile, repeat while 0 tile with question neighbors exist
ms_clear_all_0_tiles = {
	ROOT = {
		set_variable = {
			which = minesweeper_event_1_loop_exit_cond
			value = 1
		}
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = minesweeper_event_1_loop_exit_cond
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}

		# Set iteration counter
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = minesweeper_event_1_loop_exit_cond
				value = 0
			}
		}

		# Check if there are any zero provinces with question neighbors
		minesweeper_region = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = zero_mod
			}
			minesweeper_region = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_province_modifier = question_mod
						NOT = {
							province_distance = {
								who = PREV
								distance = 29
							}
						}
					}
				}

				# These are provinces with question neighbors, set their values to their flags

				# First update counter variable
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = {
						which = minesweeper_event_1_loop_exit_cond
						value = 1
					}
				}

				# Next update score variable

				owner = {
					change_variable = {
						which = score
						value = 1
					}
				}

				# Then remove question mod

				remove_province_modifier = question_mod
				ms_hide_question_tile_in_prov = yes

				# Then if block
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = zero_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = zero_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_0_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = one_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = one_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_1_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = two_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = two_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_2_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = three_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = three_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_3_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = four_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = four_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_4_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = five_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = five_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_5_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = six_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = six_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_6_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = seven_flag
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = seven_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_7_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = eight_mod
						duration = -1
					}
					ms_show_8_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				
			}
		}
	}
}

#ms menu
ms_bomb_amount = { #add/#sub
	change_variable = {
		which = bomb_total
		value = [[add]$add$][[sub]-$sub$]
	}
	[[add]
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { which = bomb_total value = 101 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = bomb_total value = 100 }
	}
	]
	[[sub]
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = bomb_total value = 0 } }
		}
		set_variable = { which = bomb_total value = 0 }
	}
	]
	country_event = {
		id = minesweeper.4
	}
}

ms_new_game = {
	custom_tooltip = ms_new_game_tooltip
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = game_in_progress_flag }
					ROOT = {
						tag = MSW
					}
					MSW = {
						NOT = { ai = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			# Initialize flag
			set_global_flag	= game_in_progress_flag

			# Set score

			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
				    which = score
				    value = 0
				}
			}

			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
				    which = flags_placed
				    value = 0
				}
			}

			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
				    which = bomb_total
				    value = 0
				}
			}

			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
				    which = bomb_count
				    value = 0
				}
			}


			# Remove old modifiers and flags
			minesweeper_region = {
				# Needs to be separate from the main modifier block
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = flag_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = flag_mod
					ms_hide_flagged_tile_in_prov = yes
				}

				# Main modifier block
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = bomb_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = bomb_mod
					ms_hide_bomb_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = zero_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = zero_mod
					ms_hide_0_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = one_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = one_mod
					ms_hide_1_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = two_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = two_mod
					ms_hide_2_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = three_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = three_mod
					ms_hide_3_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = four_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = four_mod
					ms_hide_4_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = five_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = five_mod
					ms_hide_5_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = six_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = six_mod
					ms_hide_6_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = seven_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = seven_mod
					ms_hide_7_tile_in_prov = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = eight_mod
					}
					remove_province_modifier = eight_mod
					ms_hide_8_tile_in_prov = yes
				}

				# Main flag block
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = bomb_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = bomb_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = zero_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = zero_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = one_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = one_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = two_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = two_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = three_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = three_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = four_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = four_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = five_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = five_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = six_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = six_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = seven_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = seven_flag
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = eight_flag
					}
					clr_province_flag = eight_flag
				}
			}

			MSW = {
				country_event = {
					id = minesweeper.2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
